= {&#39;type&#39; &#39;sms&#39;};<br>head(full)<br>%Switch from text to cateforical for simpler access/manipulation<br>full.type = categorical(full.type);<br>%Proportion of spam messages in the spaces.<br>%%<br>cleaned_full = full;<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;!&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;#&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;/&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;:&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;~&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms(1:5)<br>%% <br>% Default Transfromations<br>%%<br>%1. Remove numbers<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;0&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;1&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;2&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;3&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;4&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;5&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;6&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;7&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;8&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>cleaned_full.sms = strrep(cleaned_full.sms, &#39;9&#39;, &#39; &#39;);<br>%2. Remove capital letters.<br>cleaned_full.sms = lower(cleaned_full.sms);<br>%3. Remove punctuation. Just in case there is something left.<br>cleaned_full.sms = erasePunctuation(cleaned_full.sms);<br><br>cleaned_full.sms(1:5)<br>%% <br>% Make tokenized documents (bag of wrods type of thing).<br>%%<br>token_full= tokenizedDocument(string(cleaned_full.sms));<br>%3. Get rid of stop words<br>token_full = removeWords(token_full,stopWords);<br>%4. Stem the words<br>%Converting verbs to their root word. Example: &ldquo;fighting&rdquo; or &ldquo;fights&rdquo; becomes &ldquo;fight&rdquo;.<br>token_full= normalizeWords(token_full);<br>token_full(1:5)<br>%% <br>% Create bag of words and leave frequent terms only<br>%%<br>bag_full = bagOfWords(token_full);<br>%leave only those words that appear in at least 50 text messages(a little more than 1%)<br>bag_full = removeShortWords(bag_full,2);<br>bag_full= removeInfrequentWords(bag_full,40)<br>%% <br>% Create Word Frequency Matrix<br>%%<br>counts = encode(bag_full, token_full);<br>counts = counts* eye(157)<br><br>ss = repmat(&ldquo;w</em>&rdquo;, [1, 157]); % Replicate 1 time vertically, n times horizontally.;<br>all_words = strcat(ss, bag_full.Vocabulary)<br><br>%% <br>% Creating final array; type as a variable<br>%%<br>%token_full2 = tokenizedDocument(string(cleaned_full.sms));<br>%token_full2.doclength<br>% create temporary array of messages.<br>messages = cleaned_full.sms;<br><br>% add type as a variable<br>df_words = array2table(counts, &hellip;<br>    &#39;VariableNames&#39;, cellstr(all_words));<br>df_words = addvars(df_words,cleaned_full.type,&#39;Before&#39;,&#39;w_free&#39;);<br>df_words.Properties.VariableNames([1]) = {&#39;type&#39;}<br>%% <br>% Number of characters as a variable<br>%%<br>%add number of characters as a variable:<br>temp = strlength(full.sms);<br>df_words = addvars(df_words,temp,&#39;Before&#39;,&#39;type&#39;);<br>df_words.Properties.VariableNames([1]) = {&#39;nchars&#39;}<br>%% <br>% Number of upper case values<br>%%<br>% addd number of upper case vals<br>%temp = cell2table(cell(length(df_words.type),1), &#39;VariableNames&#39;, {&#39;one&#39;});<br>temp = zeros(length(df_words.type), 1);<br>for n = 1:length(df_words.type)<br>   temp(n,1) = sum( isstrprop(full.sms(n),&#39;upper&#39;) );<br>end<br>df_words = addvars(df_words,temp,&#39;Before&#39;,&#39;nchars&#39;);<br>df_words.Properties.VariableNames([1]) = {&#39;ncaps&#39;}<br>%% <br>% Number of non symbols<br>%%<br>%temp = cell2table(cell(length(df_words.type),1), &#39;VariableNames&#39;, {&#39;one&#39;});<br>temp = zeros(length(df_words.type), 1);<br>for n = 1:length(df_words.type)<br>   temp(n,1) = df_words.nchars(n) - sum( isstrprop(full.sms(n),&#39;alphanum&#39;) );<br>end<br>df_words = addvars(df_words,temp,&#39;Before&#39;,&#39;ncaps&#39;);<br>df_words.Properties.VariableNames([1]) = {&#39;nsymbs&#39;}<br>%% <br>% Done!!! Cleaning is over, the rest should be easier.<br>% <br>% Data partitioning:<br>%%<br>cv = cvpartition(df_words.type,&#39;holdout&#39;,0.20)<br>% Training set<br>train_set= df_words(training(cv),:); <br>% Test set<br>test_set = df_words(test(cv),:);<br><br>disp(&#39;Training Set&#39;)<br>tabulate(train_set.type)<br>disp(&#39;Test Set&#39;)<br>tabulate(test_set.type)<br>%% <br>% Speed Up Computations<br>%%<br>% OH YESSSS<br>parpool(2)<br>%% <br>% Trees:<br>%%<br>tree_model = fitctree(train_set, &#39;type&#39;)<br>%% <br>% Analysis for Trees:<br><br>predictions = predict(tree_model,test_set);<br>% Compute the confusion matrix<br>confusionmat(predictions, test_set.type)<br>[~,score] = resubPredict(tree_model);<br>[X,Y,T,AUC,OPTROCPT] = perfcurve(train_set.type,score(:,2),&#39;spam&#39;);<br><br>plot(X,Y)<br>hold on<br>plot(OPTROCPT(1),OPTROCPT(2),&#39;ro&#39;)<br>xlabel(&#39;False positive rate&#39;) <br>ylabel(&#39;True positive rate&#39;)<br>title(&#39;ROC Curve for Classification by Classification Trees&#39;)<br>hold off<br><br>%Area under the curve:<br>AUC<br>%Best cutoff:<br>best_cutoff = T((X==OPTROCPT(1))&amp;(Y==OPTROCPT(2)))<br>%% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% KNN: - best specificity &amp; sensitivity. K = 1<br>%%<br>knn_model_1 = fitcknn(train_set,&#39;type&#39;)<br>%% <br>% Analysis for KNN:<br><br>predictions = predict(knn_model_1,test_set);<br>% Compute the confusion matrix<br>confusionmat(predictions, test_set.type)<br><br>[~,score] = resubPredict(knn_model_1);<br>[X,Y,T,AUC,OPTROCPT] = perfcurve(train_set.type,score(:,2),&#39;spam&#39;);<br><br>plot(X,Y)<br>hold on<br>plot(OPTROCPT(1),OPTROCPT(2),&#39;ro&#39;)<br>xlabel(&#39;False positive rate&#39;) <br>ylabel(&#39;True positive rate&#39;)<br>title(&#39;ROC Curve for Classification by Classification Trees&#39;)<br>hold off<br><br>%Area under the curve:<br>AUC<br><br>%Best cutoff:<br>best_cutoff = T((X==OPTROCPT(1))&amp;(Y==OPTROCPT(2)))<br>%% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% KNN: best accuracy, sensitivity/specificity a little lower. K = 5<br>%%<br>knn_model_5 = fitcknn(train_set,&#39;type&#39;, &#39;NumNeighbors&#39;, 5)<br>%% <br>% Analysis for KNN:<br><br>predictions = predict(knn_model_5,test_set);<br>% Compute the confusion matrix<br>confusionmat(predictions, test_set.type)<br><br>[~,score] = resubPredict(knn_model_5);<br>[X,Y,T,AUC,OPTROCPT] = perfcurve(train_set.type,score(:,2),&#39;spam&#39;);<br><br>plot(X,Y)<br>hold on<br>plot(OPTROCPT(1),OPTROCPT(2),&#39;ro&#39;)<br>xlabel(&#39;False positive rate&#39;) <br>ylabel(&#39;True positive rate&#39;)<br>title(&#39;ROC Curve for Classification by Classification Trees&#39;)<br>hold off<br><br>%Area under the curve:<br>AUC<br><br>%Best cutoff:<br>best_cutoff = T((X==OPTROCPT(1))&amp;(Y==OPTROCPT(2)))<br>%% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% <br>% SVM:<br>%%<br>svm_model = fitcsvm(train_set,&#39;type&#39;)<br>%% <br>% Analysis for SVM:<br><br>predictions = predict(svm_model,test_set);<br>% Compute the confusion
